<username>Erik Brodin< /username><Date>1531996294299< /Date><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
I was in at the same time as reviewer John Munoz (Villanueva). We walked in at the same exact time on Valentine's Day morning, yesterday. This florist is very busy for good reason. Luis, half of the husband-wife duo running the show, explained that on Valentine's Day, walk-in orders are not feasible unless you are willing to wait. He reasoned that there were over a hundred orders ahead of us and it would not be fair to everyone who already ordered and paid weeks or even months in advance. This guy was not happy with this info and stormed off in a big huff. How can you review a business if you haven't even been a customer before? I know they would never turn away a potential customer on any other day. His review, which fails to mention critical details, should not even be posted up as it is in no way accurate for this business.

Anyway, I was happy to wait. There is a reason Darling's Holm & Olson is so busy. Aida always has the best arrangement designs and freshest flowers, and the locals (and plenty not-so-local) know it. My family and friends have been customers for at least 20 years and probably more. Hands down this is the only florist worth visiting in Los Angeles. Any other day I know I can expect to walk in here and within 15 minutes, have the most fragrant, freshest flowers filling my car with their enticing aroma. I don't know how anyone could give this place less than 5 stars!<//review>

< Review>
Got there close to closing time, they were friendly and did not rush us. It's a family owned business, if you are into supporting local businesses and like Indian food like we do please give them a try.

We started with 2 appetizers that complimented each other: fried veggies ( Gobhi Pakora) and a cauliflower dish ( Manchurian Gobhi). The sauce for the cauliflower dish was excellent and I dipped the fried veggies in it, it was superb!!

For the main dish we ordered the chefs choice lamb and the shrimp tanduri. Both were very good. Combine that with excellent hospitality and you have a winning combination for mod week lunch experience.

Will definitely come back with the greater family. I just hope these guys can survive the Covid outbreak.< /Review>

< Text>
Well we finally found a great Indian Restaurant, and it's near home in Rancho Bernardo! Super nice gentleman on the phone and at the desk. We started with Aloo Samosa..perfectly stuffed and fried with excellent dipping chutneys. Our main courses were Chicken Tikka Masala...perfect from taste to heat and Lamb Rogan Josh was perfect as well with very tender lamb. Delicious Naan and a small aromatic Rice Pudding so good with cardamom. Coming from New York, we're quite spoiled when it comes to ethnic restaurants, San Diego has quite often been a let down, especially Indian food. If you love Indian Food, look no further. If you have a desire to try it for the first time, THIS IS THE PLACE!! Thank You Sher E Punjab!!<//Text>

< Text>
This review is for the brand new Rancho Bernardo location. Absolutely delicious! I went to the lunch buffet and it is sort of a soft opening right now because it is not officially open yet and the old name with the old owner sign is still up, but these are new owners and they are the same as the original Sher-E-Punjab, And the food is absolutely delicious! Very friendly and kind and respectful service. I did not feel uneasy eating alone as a woman. They had a wonderful variety perfectly seasoned Northern Indian dishes. They did have some Southern Indian options as well, but they are Northern Indian, themselves. The basmati rice was fresh, and did not taste like it had been sitting around all day. The price of the all-you-can-eat lunch buffet is very affordable. While I do eat meat sometimes, I primarily I'm vegetarian or even vegan, and they had absolutely a delicious variety of vegetarian friendly food! They make their own cheese there, And I tried the paneer tikka. Very perfectly seasoned, and their homemade cheese is light and fluffy. Also, unlike many all you can eat buffets I have been to, this seemed very fresh and the food was not overly salty. It was just perfectly seasoned. Another standout dish was the veggie korma, which is one of my favorite dishes, and I will say this is the best veggie korma I have ever tasted. The restaurant is very clean, and I will definitely go back and bring my friends. Another thing about the service, it was just right. If you needed someone they were available, so you never felt like you were being ignored, but there was no hovering either, which was great! Really fantastic, and I can't wait until the location on Bernardo Center Drive is officially open and known to the public!<//Text>

<userid>111192904613282266427< /userid><Name>CJ Hardman</Name><Time>1543986088129<//Time>< rate>
5<//rate>
< Review>
My favorite Indian place in San Diego.  Lunch and dinner are traditional and delicious.  Food is traditional Indian style, with whole spices in food for strong traditional flavors (people, if you find a cinnamon sticks in your food just set it  to side of the plate and keep eating).

Love the buffet, yes it's all you can eat.  Take your time, enjoy the sights, scents, and Indian atmosphere.  Don't waste-- you can take a bit, and come back for more if you like next time.

Traditionally seasoned ragout-style dishes, Spinach paneer, Tikka Masala, usually a dhal, vegetarian and meat (chicken, lamb, sometimes seafood) choices.   Seasoned with mouth watering mustard seed, cumin, fennel, peppers, magnificent cardamom!  If you're lucky on a weekday there will be gulab jamun those deliciously cardmom and rose spiced milk dough balls floating in sugar for desert!<//Review>

We all know how google maps work when searching for a place. Though, don't let high reviews fool you, always visit them to see the location and talk with the staff in person.  Be kind and personable and you'll find out how they care about their work. Happy employees make for a happier business.  Anyhow.....

Upon researching online and visiting different Self Storage websites.... I've noticed there is a lot of online deals to be had right on their websites.  I narrowed it down to 4 different Self Storages. They all have very competitive prices online.  Though, one is way cheaper but does not compare to how well the other 3 maintain their properties.

Of the 4, I was able to narrow it down to just 2 Self Storages.  They both had great customer service, clean facilities, excellent security features and knew their business well.  Very close in rental prices online too.

Richard was helping me. Scott the manager, was helping another customer and I couldn't help but listen on the side. Great and awesome people!

Richard was able to answer all my questions and then some.  Security is top notch here.
- Gated with keypad
- Individually alarmed units
- Vented outside air into their facility. I couldn't find a climate controlled Self Storage around due to my time constraint and wanted to stay in carlsbad by Palomar Airport.
- They do use a special kind of lock that is set inside of the roll up doors with star keys. No hinges on their doors for padlocks. Another added security feature.  I don't mind.... I'll use StorQuest again in a heartbeat.
- Customer restroom. Well taken care of
- Surveillance system
- Free carts to use to move your goods
- Large Elevators
- Main building has a covered loading dock
- Well maintained
- Clean. Inside and out. Just a beautiful location
- Boxes and accessories if you need to buy.
- Go ask them about different leasing times.
- They do have different tiers on access times.  No 24 hour access.

- Though you have to buy storage rental insurance from them or provide your own.  An added cost, but I didn't mind for the price I was given.

Do check them out if you are looking! Check out their website first for availability and call if you have any questions about StorQuest. I feel very safe here and for my stuff.

I've added photos and a few videos of this place

< text>
Over the years (and in various locales), I‚Äôve had a number of storage units, and I can say without a doubt that my experience at StorQuest - Carlsbad / Campbell has been one of the best, if not the best, storage-unit experience I‚Äôve had.

First off, this place is CLEAN! Other places just don‚Äôt come close to the attractiveness and cleanliness of this place. And second, and high up on the list: both the manager, Scott Jedlick and his assistant, Richard offer great customer service. Prior to getting this storage unit, I checked out several places (over the phone and in person). During this period (person and phone), I talked to both Scott and Richard and they explained things well and came across as very professional, plus the rate I was quoted was extremely competitive. I got a 10‚Äô X 15‚Äô unit with StorQuest that was less expensive that some other places‚Äô 10‚Äô X 10‚Äô units.

I was a little hesitant about a second story unit, but Richard pointed out the dollies around the facility and with being able to park right next to the elevator (and with my unit being close to the elevator), I found that my initial fears were unwarranted. It was easy to access my unit, and to move things in and out of it.

At this place, they have you purchase a cylinder lock (~ $20.00 plus tax) to lock your unit. This is a very secure type of lock! In the past, at another storage facility, I had my lock cut open and my unit broken into. When I told this to StorQuest manager, Scott, he explained how secure and virtually-tamper proof these cylinder locks are.

There was one more thing that I really liked about this place: after punching in your code at the entrance, the buildings are arranged so that you drive (in one direction) in a big square and exit at the other side (where you again punch in your code for the exit gate to open). This seemed safer to me than cars and trucks coming and going in different directions, and like I said before, I was able to park right next to the elevator in my building. The driving space/path between the buildings was quite adequate so that cars and trucks could easily pass around cars parked to the side.

I had my unit at StorQuest for about 6 months until I could arrange to move my items out, and Scott was extremely helpful on my last day there (extending my gate access hours by two hours to accommodate my needs). If I ever need a storage unit again, and am in this North County area, I‚Äôd definitely use StorQuest - Carlsbad / Campbell again!< /text>
